              Sisoft Healthcare Information Systems
Founded in 1987, Sisoft has been at the forefront of web‑native, modular health IT. Our solutions are designed to streamline every aspect of healthcare delivery and empower professionals with actionable insights.

Flagship Platform:

SisoHIS – a fully integrated Hospital Information Management System that digitizes clinical, administrative, financial, and support workflows

Modular architecture allows tailored deployments and rapid scaling

Global Reach:

Deployed in 1,200+ healthcare organizations across Europe, Asia, and Africa

Serves facilities ranging from small clinics to multi‑hospital networks

Advanced Capabilities:

AI‑driven analytics for predictive insights and operational optimization

Mobile‑first design supporting on‑the‑go access and decision‑making

Seamless interoperability with national e‑health systems, HL7/FHIR, and third‑party applications

Certifications &amp; Compliance:

ISO 9001 Quality Management

ISO 27001 Information Security

HIMSS Analytics Stage 6 &amp; 7

Common Criteria CC 4+

Our Mission:
Through continuous innovation and strategic partnerships, Sisoft empowers healthcare teams to enhance patient safety, improve efficiency, and deliver truly data‑driven care.

    <div data-id="entire-feed-card-link" class="relative">

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌐 End-to-End Hospital Information Systems with SisoHIS
At Sisoft, we’ve delivered a secure, scalable, and interoperable hospital automation platform that powers 1,000+ hospitals worldwide. Our All-in-One HIS, LIS, PACS, ERP solution transforms healthcare into a smarter, safer, and more connected ecosystem.

    🔒 Security &amp; Standards
          ✅ CC EAL4+: Certified system security
          ⚙️ SPICE Level 5: Advanced software engineering capability
          🔗 IHE &amp; HL7: Seamless interoperability with global standards

    🏥 Clinical Excellence
          🧪 Integrated Laboratory, Radiology &amp; PACS
         🛡️ Patient Safety: Risk-reducing workflows &amp; error-prevention mechanisms
         💉 Specialized modules: ICU, Emergency, Organ Transplant, IVF

    ⚡ Operational Strength
         🚫 No third-party software needed
         🌍 OS &amp; Browser Independent
         🔄 Offline Working Capability
         🗣️ Multi-language: 16 languages (EN, FR, ES, AR, RU, …)

    📈 Scalability &amp; Flexibility
          🏢 Chain-hospital solutions for private groups
          🏛️ National / City-wide centralized hospital networks
          📜 Adapted to local regulations &amp; medical practices
          ☁️ Cloud-ready for scalable deployment
With decades of experience, SisoHIS ensures hospitals operate safer, faster, and smarter – without limits.</p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌐 SisoPortal - Patient portal integrated with SisoHIS

🧑⚕️ Personal Health Management
  • Access to all health records (reports, discharge summaries, test results, images)
  • Overview of past consultations and treatments
  • Chronic disease tracking (diabetes, hypertension, etc.)

📅 Online Appointment Management
  • Easy booking by doctor or specialty
  • Quick cancellation or rescheduling
  • Smart reminders via SMS, email, or mobile app

🧪 Laboratory &amp; Imaging Results
  • Instant online access to lab results
  • Radiology image viewing with DICOM integration
  • Test explanations and comments from physicians

💊 Prescription &amp; Medication Tracking
  • Direct access to electronic prescriptions
  • Clear dosage and medication instructions

💬 Doctor–Patient Communication
  • Secure encrypted messaging
  • Direct information notes and follow-ups from physicians

📚 Information &amp; Education
  • Reliable medical content on diseases and treatments
  • Educational videos, brochures, and guides
  • Lifestyle and wellness recommendations

🔔 Personalized Notifications
  • Reminders for upcoming appointments
  • Alerts when lab results are ready
  • Notifications on treatment plan updates

🔒 Data Security &amp; Privacy
  • Strong user authentication (2FA, SMS verification, etc.)
  • Full compliance with GDPR, CC, and KVKK
  • Encrypted data transfer for maximum safety

🌍 Multilingual support in 15 languages (English, French, Spanish, Russian, Arabic, and more)

💻 Fully integrated with SisoHIS – seamless hospital–patient connectivity

📧 Contact: <a class="link" href="mailto:sisoft@sisoft.us?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>sisoft@sisoft.us</a>
🌐 Website: <a class="link" href="http://www.sisoft.us?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>www.sisoft.us</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌐 Introducing SisoPMA – Infertility Module (IVF Module)
SisoPMA is a comprehensive infertility treatment solution, fully integrated with SisoHIS for seamless data flow and centralized hospital management.

🎯 Target Audience:
Maternity hospitals, training &amp; research hospitals, and university hospitals.

🔹 Key Features:

Infertility Treatment Application – End-to-end patient journey management.

 ✔️ Clinical Evaluation – Comprehensive medical assessments.

 ✔️ Examination – Structured patient examination workflows.

 ✔️ Etiological Assessment – For both female and male patients.

 ✔️ Tank Module – Cryogenic storage management.

 ✔️ Stimulation Protocols – Controlled ovarian stimulation tracking.

 ✔️ Cryo Module – Embryo, oocyte, and sperm freezing management.

 ✔️ Treatment Monitoring – Real-time treatment follow-up.

 ✔️ Ovum and Sperm Tracking – Secure and traceable sample management.

🔒 Security &amp; Compliance:

 ✔️ Fully integrated with SisoHIS, HIS, LIS, PACS, and ERP modules.

 ✔️ Patient data sharing according to user authorization levels.

 ✔️ Common Criteria EAL4+ compliant.

 ✔️ SPICE Level 5 certified development processes.

 ✔️ Secure, cloud-ready, and scalable for national-level deployments.

🌍 Multilingual Support:
Supports 15 languages, including English, French, Spanish, Arabic ready for global operations.

💡 Designed for institutions where precision, patient safety, and regulatory compliance are top priorities.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🔒 SisoHIS – Centralized Hospital Automation for Military and High-Security Health Institutions
Designed for:
Military hospitals and high-security healthcare institutions requiring isolated (closed-loop) operations, strict data control, and centralized governance.
🌐 Centralized System Architecture
Operates on a single server and unified database schema.
Ideal for multiple hospitals operating under one authority.
Compatible with VPN, Cloud, Local Network, or Public Internet infrastructure.
📊 Smart Access &amp; Authority-Controlled Data Sharing
Patient data is securely accessible based on user authorization levels.
Authorized staff can view relevant patient records regardless of originating hospital, in compliance with data privacy.
Ministries or central health authorities can monitor hospital-specific or consolidated data instantly, including real-time statistics.
📍 Nationwide Disease Surveillance
Identify regional trends:
Which diseases or symptoms are prevalent in which regions, cities, or hospitals.
Real-time monitoring to support public health response.
🔐 Security, Compliance &amp; Traceability
Fully compliant with Common Criteria EAL4+ certification.
Developed under SPICE Level 5 software maturity standards.
End-to-end traceable audit trail, with:
Record observation logs
Access tracking
Action blocking or locking capabilities
🧩 Scalable &amp; Flexible Integration
Easily extendable for national coverage.
Plug-and-play integration with e-Health systems, insurance platforms, and legacy modules.
🌍 Multilingual &amp; Localization-Ready
Supports 15 languages including:
English, French, Spanish, Arabic, and Russian
Fully adaptable to local regulations and medical workflows.
💼 Ideal For:
Defense &amp; Military Health Institutions
Public Health Authorities
Government Health Projects
Large-Scale Multi-Hospital Networks

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌐 SisoICU – Integrated Critical Care Management System

Powering Intensive Care in Over 100 Hospitals Across the Globe
🔹 Advanced ICU Workflow Integration
SisoICU is a dedicated Intensive Care Unit (ICU) module designed to seamlessly integrate with our all-in-one hospital solution:
SisoHIS (Hospital Information System), SisoLIS (Laboratory Information System), SisoPACS (Imaging), and SisoERP (Enterprise Resource Planning) modules.
🔹 Real-Time Device Connectivity
SisoICU is interoperable with a wide range of ICU medical devices. Vital data such as heart rate, oxygen saturation, ventilation metrics, and infusion rates are automatically captured and displayed in real time across dashboards and patient monitoring panels.
🔹 Tailored for Local Regulations
From Europe to the Middle East and Africa, SisoICU adapts to each country’s legal and medical regulations, ensuring localized compliance and usability in every deployment.
🔹 Secure, Scalable, and Cloud-Ready
Built on a secure and scalable architecture, SisoICU is cloud-ready and optimized for centralized server models where multiple hospitals can operate on a single database schema.
🔹 Proven Standards of Excellence
Our development adheres to the highest international standards:
✔️ Common Criteria EAL4+ certified
✔️ SPICE Level 5 development maturity
🔹 Multilingual and Globally Adaptable
Available in 15 languages, including French, English, Arabic, and Spanish, ensuring user-friendly experiences for international healthcare teams.
💡 Why SisoICU?
✔️ Real-time clinical insights for critical decision-making
✔️ Streamlined communication between ICU and hospital-wide systems
✔️ Enhanced patient safety through automation and accuracy
✔️ Trusted by hospitals with the most demanding intensive care environments
📍 SisoICU: Because Every Second Counts in Critical Car.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌍 SisoHIS – Digital Health Infrastructure for Francophone Nations
With nearly 40 years of experience in healthcare IT, SisoHIS delivers a centralized, scalable, and secure hospital automation solution that is already live in three different countries, each adapted to its national legislation and medical practices.
Designed specifically for Francophone regions, SisoHIS combines flexibility, multilingual support, and international standards to modernize hospital operations across borders.

📌 Proven Deployments Across Multiple Countries
Active in 3 different countries with customized versions
Adapted to each country’s legal framework, clinical protocols, and operational workflows
Trusted by public and military hospitals

🧩 All-in-One Integrated Platform
HIS – Hospital Information System
LIS – Laboratory Information System
PACS – Radiology and Imaging
ERP – Enterprise Resource Planning Modules (Finance, HR, Inventory, Procurement)
No third-party integration needed — everything is natively built, fully integrated, and highly interoperable.

🛡 Built on Global Standards and Robust Security
Common Criteria EAL4+ certified architecture
SPICE Level 5 compliant development lifecycle
Audit trail on all table-level modifications
User activity tracking and role-based logging
Offline mode ensures operational continuity during internet or power outages
Fully cloud-ready and horizontally scalable for national-level deployments

🌐 Centralized Management with Distributed Access
All connected hospitals run on a single database schema and central server
Access can be configured per hospital, per user, or unified across institutions
Ideal for national eHealth platforms, MOH supervision, and regional health networks

🗣️ Multilingual by Design
Available in French, English, Spanish, Arabic — and 15+ languages in total
Interface and printouts localized per country and user profile
Supports Unicode, right-to-left (RTL) scripts, and medical terminology dictionaries in multiple languages

🚀 Why SisoHIS?
Designed for real-world hospital needs
Trusted in military, public, private and university hospitals
A powerful solution for countries aiming to digitize and standardize healthcare delivery

📣 Discover how SisoHIS is transforming healthcare across Francophone nations — one country at a time.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌐 Centralized Hospital Information System – Powered by SisoHIS
Sisoft is proud to present a secure, scalable, and multilingual hospital automation solution based on a centralized server architecture.
🏥 Widespread Implementation
Our system is currently in active use in:
✔️ 10 provinces across Turkey
✔️ 1 central hospital in Pakistan
✔️ 1 major hospital in Azerbaijan
In one city alone, 23 hospitals serve 65,000+ patients daily, all operating on a single central server.
🔐 Role-Based Access
Users can only access data from their own hospital unless granted additional permissions.
Authorized personnel can view data from individual hospitals or combined datasets, depending on their access level.
🧩 All-in-One Integrated System
Includes:
✅ Hospital Information System (HIS)
✅ Laboratory Information System (LIS)
✅ Picture Archiving and Communication System (PACS)
✅ Enterprise Resource Planning (ERP) modules
🛡️ Standards &amp; Security
Fully compliant with Common Criteria EAL4+
Developed in line with SPICE Level 5 processes
Secure, cloud-ready, and scalable for national-level deployments
🌍 Multilingual Support
Supports 15 languages, including English, French, Spanish, and Arabic — ready for global operations.

      </div>
  
        
      </div>

      
            
            
  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌟 High-Security Military Hospital Solutions – SisoHIS
At Sisoft, we lead the digital transformation in military healthcare with our successfully implemented automation systems in Turkey and Algeria.
 
🔒 Military-Grade Security Standards
Software architecture developed in accordance with SPICE methodology
Infrastructure compatible with Common Criteria EAL4+ certification level
Full-function operation over closed network structures (VPN, LAN)
Encrypted transmission and offline data backup to prevent data leakage
 
⚖️ Advanced Authorization &amp; Access Control
Detailed individual and group-based authorization
Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)
Audit trail on all module and operation levels
Local permission control even in offline mode
 
🚀 Comprehensive Modules &amp; Offline Capabilities
Integration of HIS, LIS, PACS, ERP, and e-Archive modules
Data entry, registration, and synchronization in offline mode
Full compliance in disconnected environments like field hospitals
 
🌐 International Experience &amp; Large-Scale Success
Algeria Military Mother and Child Hospital: 100% offline-capable, closed-system operation
Dozens of successful military hospital implementations in Turkey
Domestic R&amp;D, local support, and stable long-term partnerships
 
🌍 Open to New Strategic Partnerships
We welcome new collaborations with institutions in need of secure, offline, and integrated military hospital information systems.
 
Let’s build a more secure healthcare ecosystem together.
